protocol implementation is structured around an adapter pattern with a unified template-based mux system supporting both State-of-the-World (SotW) and Delta modes.\\n\\n## Core Adapter: GrpcSubscriptionImpl\\nThe GrpcSubscriptionImpl class (source/extensions/config_subscription/grpc/grpc_subscription_impl.h/cc) serves as the main adapter, converting typed Subscription interfaces to untyped GrpcMux operations. It handles per-xDS API stats and logging while managing subscription lifecycle through the GrpcMux interface.\\n\\n## Legacy Implementation - Two Separate Muxers\\nEnvoy initially had two distinct implementations:\\n\\n1. **SotW Mode (GrpcMuxImpl)**: The legacy State-of-the-World implementation in source/extensions/config_subscription/grpc/grpc_mux_impl.h/cc manages subscriptions using full resource snapshots with DiscoveryRequest/DiscoveryResponse messages.\\n\\n2. **Delta Mode (NewGrpcMuxImpl)**: The legacy Delta xDS implementation in source/extensions/config_subscription/grpc/new_grpc_mux_impl.h/cc manages subscriptions with resource-level updates using DeltaDiscoveryRequest/DeltaDiscoveryResponse messages.\\n\\n## Unified Template Architecture - XdsMux\\nTo converge these implementations, Envoy introduced a generic template-based system in the XdsMux namespace (source/extensions/config_subscription/grpc/xds_mux/grpc_mux_impl.h/cc):\\n\\nThe template GrpcMuxImpl<S, F, RQ, RS> is parameterized by:\\n- **S**: SubscriptionState type (SotwSubscriptionState or DeltaSubscriptionState)\\n- **F**: SubscriptionStateFactory type (SotwSubscriptionStateFactory or DeltaSubscriptionStateFactory)\\n- **RQ**: Request type (DiscoveryRequest or DeltaDiscoveryRequest)\\n- **RS**: Response type (DiscoveryResponse or DeltaDiscoveryResponse)\\n\\nTwo concrete specializations are provided:\\n- **GrpcMuxSotw**: Specialization for SotW protocol using SotwSubscriptionState\\n- **GrpcMuxDelta**: Specialization for Delta protocol using DeltaSubscriptionState\\n\\n## Subscription State Protocol Handling\\nThe xds_mux directory contains abstract and concrete subscription state classes that encapsulate protocol-specific logic:\\n\\n- **BaseSubscriptionState** (source/extensions/config_subscription/grpc/xds_mux/subscription_state.h): Abstract template base class handling common protocol concerns like TTL management and response handling.\\n\\n- **SotwSubscriptionState** (source/extensions/config_subscription/grpc/xds_mux/sotw_subscription_state.h/cc): Implements SotW-specific logic including version tracking and full resource snapshot management.\\n\\n- **DeltaSubscriptionState** (source/extensions/config_subscription/grpc/xds_mux/delta_subscription_state.h/cc): Implements Delta-specific logic including per-resource versioning and incremental updates.\\n\\n## Configuration Selection - GrpcConfigSubscriptionFactory\\nThe factory pattern in source/extensions/config_subscription/grpc/grpc_subscription_factory.h/cc makes the selection between modes:\\n\\n- **GrpcConfigSubscriptionFactory**: Selects between GrpcMuxImpl (legacy) or XdsMux::GrpcMuxSotw (unified) based on the \\\"envoy.reloadable_features.unified_mux\\\" runtime feature flag.\\n\\n- **DeltaGrpcConfigSubscriptionFactory**: Selects between NewGrpcMuxImpl (legacy) or XdsMux::GrpcMuxDelta (unified) based on the same runtime feature flag.\\n\\n- **AdsConfigSubscriptionFactory**: Uses the aggregated discovery service (ADS) mux.\\n\\nThe factories create GrpcSubscriptionImpl instances wrapping the appropriate mux implementation, enabling runtime switching between the legacy dual-mux approach and the new unified template-based implementation.\"\n}\n"},"caller":{"type":"direct"}}],"stop_reason":null,"stop_sequence":null,"usage":{"input_tokens":11,"cache_creation_input_tokens":2831,"cache_read_input_tokens":67498,"cache_creation":{"ephemeral_5m_input_tokens":0,"ephemeral_1h_input_tokens":2831},"output_tokens":4,"service_tier":"standard","inference_geo":"not_available"},"context_management":null},"parent_tool_use_id":null,"session_id":"84485c0c-7ec7-42e6-9e0e-cc3eba93ff33","uuid":"151347d2-8e73-4289-9e0f-6e79029b2df1"}
